System Profiles |  |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
Foundational (F) | 97 ACRs | Single-purpose text agents, internal-only, no tool access, no sensitive data. Startup MVPs, internal FAQ chatbots. |  |  |  |  |  | 
Standard (S) | 215 ACRs | Multi-turn agents with tool access, customer-facing, handles business data. Enterprise workflow automation, customer service agents. |  |  |  |  |  | 
Advanced (A) | 368 ACRs | Multi-agent systems, multimodal, high-stakes decisions, regulated data. Financial services AI, healthcare AI, government AI. |  |  |  |  |  | 
Comprehensive (C) | 410 ACRs | All systems including autonomous physical systems, CBRN-adjacent, critical infrastructure, autonomous vehicles. |  |  |  |  |  |

 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
Certification Levels |  |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
Level 1: Foundation | Evidence inspection + policy review. Self-assessment option for Foundational profile. 3-4 week Express path. |  |  |  | 12 months | Annual |  | 
Level 2: Operational | L1 + automated testing + operational evidence over 6-month window + third-party AVB assessment. |  |  |  | 12 months | Semi-annual re-test, annual re-certification |  | 
Level 3: Comprehensive | L2 + continuous SDK monitoring + adversarial red-team testing + independent third-party evaluation. |  |  |  | 12 months | Continuous via SDK + quarterly formal |  |

ACR-1.01 | Domain 1: Autonomy Scope Definition | The system SHALL maintain a machine-readable operational boundary specification document that enumerates all permitted action classes. | EI | Boundary specification document with version control. | 1 | 4 | B | NIST AI RMF Map 1.1; EU AI Act Art. 9 | F,S,A,C | Boundary specification document with version control. | System Integrity | NIST AI RMF Map 1.1; EU AI Act Art. 9 | Annual | Documentation review + policy inspection | Documentation audit | Y
ACR-1.02 | Domain 1: Autonomy Scope Definition | The system SHALL maintain a human-readable operational boundary specification document accessible to all authorized stakeholders. | EI | Human-readable boundary document with distribution records. | 1 | 3 | C | NIST AI RMF Map 1.1; ISO/IEC 42001 A.6.1 | S,A,C | Human-readable boundary document with distribution records. | System Integrity | NIST AI RMF Map 1.1; ISO/IEC 42001 A.6.1 | At-Certification | Documentation review + policy inspection | Documentation audit | Y
ACR-1.03 | Domain 1: Autonomy Scope Definition | All permitted action classes SHALL be enumerated with specificity sufficient for automated enforcement. | EI+AT | Action class enumeration document; automated enforcement test results. | 1 | 4 | B | NIST AI RMF Map 1.2 | F,S,A,C | Action class enumeration document; automated enforcement test results. | System Integrity | NIST AI RMF Map 1.2 | Annual | Basic automated testing + evidence review | Comprehensive automated testing + documentation audit | Y
ACR-1.04 | Domain 1: Autonomy Scope Definition | All restricted and prohibited action classes SHALL be explicitly defined with equal specificity to permitted actions. | EI | Restricted action specification document. | 1 | 4 | B | NIST AI RMF Map 1.2; EU AI Act Art. 9 | F,S,A,C | Restricted action specification document. | System Integrity | NIST AI RMF Map 1.2; EU AI Act Art. 9 | Annual | Documentation review + policy inspection | Documentation audit | Y

ACR-5.01 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system operator SHALL maintain a documented AI input data policy specifying how customer, user, and third-party data is used for training, fine-tuning, inference, and caching — including opt-in/opt-out mechanisms and retention schedules. | EI | Published AI input data policy with version control and distribution records. | 1 | 5 | B | NIST AI RMF Map 1.5; EU AI Act Art. 10; ISO 42001 A.7.3; OWASP LLM-06; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | F,S,A,C | AI Input Data Policy (published document); customer notification records; opt-out mechanism documentation | Information Governance | NIST AI RMF Map 1.5; EU AI Act Art. 10; ISO 42001 A.7.3; OWASP LLM-06 | Annual | Policy document review; opt-out mechanism exists | Policy + customer notification logs + opt-out audit trail + annual policy review records | P
ACR-5.02 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system operator SHALL maintain a documented AI output data policy specifying ownership of generated outputs, usage rights, downstream restrictions, and deletion procedures. | EI | Published AI output data policy with version control. | 1 | 4 | B | NIST AI RMF Map 1.5; EU AI Act Art. 13; ISO 42001 A.7.4; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | F,S,A,C | AI Output Data Policy (published document); terms of service referencing output ownership | Information Governance | NIST AI RMF Map 1.5; EU AI Act Art. 13; ISO 42001 A.7.4 | Annual | Policy document review | Policy + terms of service audit + downstream restriction enforcement logs | P
ACR-5.03 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL classify all data it processes according to a documented sensitivity taxonomy (e.g., public, internal, confidential, restricted) and apply handling controls proportional to classification level. | EI+AT | Data classification taxonomy and handling matrix; automated classification test results. | 1 | 4 | B | NIST AI RMF Map 3.2; ISO 27001 A.5.12; NIST SP 800-53 RA-2; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | Data classification taxonomy document; handling controls matrix; classification enforcement test results | Information Governance | NIST AI RMF Map 3.2; ISO 27001 A.5.12; NIST SP 800-53 RA-2 | Annual | Taxonomy document + handling matrix review | Taxonomy + automated classification testing + enforcement verification | P
ACR-5.04 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system operator SHALL maintain a documented data flow map identifying all data ingress, processing, storage, and egress points — including third-party services, caching layers, and telemetry pipelines. | EI | Data flow diagram with all integration points documented. | 1 | 4 | C | NIST AI RMF Map 1.1; EU AI Act Art. 11; NIST SP 800-53 PM-5; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | Data flow architecture diagram; integration point inventory; third-party data processor list | Information Governance | NIST AI RMF Map 1.1; EU AI Act Art. 11; NIST SP 800-53 PM-5 | At-Certification | Data flow diagram review | Diagram + integration point verification + third-party audit | P
ACR-5.05 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL limit data collection and retention to the minimum necessary for the authorized task, enforced by configurable data access scoping tied to user roles and operational context. | AT+EI | Data minimization configuration; role-based access scope documentation. | 1 | 4 | B | NIST AI RMF Manage 3.1; EU AI Act Art. 10(5); OECD AI Principle 1.4; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | F,S,A,C | Data minimization policy; role-based scoping configuration; data access audit logs | Information Governance | NIST AI RMF Manage 3.1; EU AI Act Art. 10(5); OECD AI Principle 1.4 | Quarterly | Policy review + configuration documentation | Policy + automated access scope testing + data retention audit | P
ACR-5.06 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL support user consent management including opt-out mechanisms for data usage, data portability requests, and verifiable deletion of user-specific data. | AT+EI | Consent management interface; deletion verification test results. | 1 | 4 | B | EU AI Act Art. 10; GDPR Art. 17; CCPA Sec. 1798.105; OECD AI Principle 1.3; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | Consent management UI/API documentation; opt-out workflow test results; deletion verification evidence | Information Governance | EU AI Act Art. 10; GDPR Art. 17; CCPA Sec. 1798.105; OECD AI Principle 1.3 | Quarterly | Consent mechanism documentation + opt-out workflow demo | Consent mechanism + automated deletion testing + portability test + audit trail | P
ACR-5.07 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL enforce documented data retention schedules with automated purging and SHALL demonstrate verifiable deletion of expired data including from caches, logs, and backup systems. | AT+EI | Retention schedule; automated purge configuration; deletion verification. | 1 | 4 | B | NIST SP 800-53 SI-12; ISO 27001 A.8.10; GDPR Art. 5(1)(e); CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | Data retention schedule; automated purge job configuration; cache/log/backup deletion verification evidence | Information Governance | NIST SP 800-53 SI-12; ISO 27001 A.8.10; GDPR Art. 5(1)(e) | Quarterly | Retention schedule document + purge configuration review | Schedule + automated purge testing + cache/backup deletion verification | P
ACR-5.08 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL provide clear disclosure to end users when they are interacting with an AI system rather than a human, except where the AI nature is already obvious from context. | EI+AT | AI interaction disclosure implementation; user interface screenshots. | 1 | 3 | C | EU AI Act Art. 52; California SB 1001; OECD AI Principle 1.3 | S,A,C | AI disclosure implementation evidence; user-facing notification screenshots or recordings | Information Governance | EU AI Act Art. 52; California SB 1001; OECD AI Principle 1.3 | At-Certification | Disclosure implementation review | Disclosure + user testing + multi-channel verification | P
ACR-5.09 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL implement automated detection and prevention of personally identifiable information in outputs, logs, telemetry, cached data, and error messages, with configurable sensitivity thresholds. | AT | PII detection test results across all output channels. | 1 | 5 | B | NIST AI RMF Manage 2.2; OWASP LLM-06; NIST SP 800-53 SI-15; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | F,S,A,C | PII detection test suite results; false positive/negative rates; threshold configuration documentation | Information Governance | NIST AI RMF Manage 2.2; OWASP LLM-06; NIST SP 800-53 SI-15 | Quarterly | PII detection test results on sample outputs | Comprehensive PII testing across all channels + adversarial PII extraction testing + continuous monitoring | P
ACR-5.10 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | In shared or multi-customer environments, the system SHALL enforce strict isolation preventing any customer's data from appearing in another customer's inputs, outputs, context, or model state. | AT+HS | Cross-customer isolation test suite results. | 1 | 5 | A | NIST SP 800-53 SC-4; CSA AICM DS-02; OWASP LLM-06; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | Tenant isolation architecture diagram; database schema showing namespace separation; cross-customer contamination test results | Information Governance | NIST SP 800-53 SC-4; CSA AICM DS-02; OWASP LLM-06 | Quarterly | Architecture review + basic isolation testing | Architecture + comprehensive isolation testing + adversarial cross-tenant extraction testing | P
ACR-5.11 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL prevent data from prior sessions, conversations, or user contexts from leaking into subsequent interactions with different users or in different operational contexts. | AT | Context isolation test results. | 1 | 5 | B | NIST AI RMF Measure 2.6; OWASP LLM-06; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | F,S,A,C | Session isolation test results; context leakage test suite; memory/state management documentation | Information Governance | NIST AI RMF Measure 2.6; OWASP LLM-06 | Quarterly | Basic context isolation testing | Comprehensive session isolation + adversarial context extraction + continuous monitoring | P
ACR-5.12 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | Operational logs, telemetry streams, and monitoring data SHALL be sanitized to prevent exposure of sensitive input data, PII, or confidential business information. | AT+EI | Log sanitization configuration; sample sanitized log output. | 1 | 4 | B | NIST SP 800-53 AU-3; ISO 27001 A.8.11; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | F,S,A,C | Log sanitization pipeline documentation; sample sanitized logs; PII scan of telemetry output | Information Governance | NIST SP 800-53 AU-3; ISO 27001 A.8.11 | Quarterly | Sanitization config review + sample log inspection | Config + automated PII scanning of log streams + telemetry audit | P
ACR-5.13 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL enforce security controls on all caching mechanisms, temporary storage, and intermediate processing buffers to prevent data exposure through side-channel or timing attacks. | AT | Cache security test results; side-channel analysis. | 2 | 4 | B | NIST SP 800-53 SC-28; MITRE ATLAS AML.T0024; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | A,C | Cache security architecture; encryption-at-rest evidence for temporary storage; side-channel test report | Information Governance | NIST SP 800-53 SC-28; MITRE ATLAS AML.T0024 | Annual | N/A (L2+ only) | Cache security testing + encryption verification + side-channel analysis | P
ACR-5.14 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL implement safeguards to prevent leakage of intellectual property, trade secrets, and confidential business information through outputs, logs, telemetry, or error messages. | AT+EI | IP protection test results; output filtering configuration. | 1 | 5 | B | NIST AI RMF Manage 2.2; OWASP LLM-06; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | IP protection policy; output filtering configuration; IP leakage test results across output channels | Information Governance | NIST AI RMF Manage 2.2; OWASP LLM-06 | Quarterly | IP protection policy + basic output filtering review | Policy + adversarial IP extraction testing + continuous output monitoring | P
ACR-5.15 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL implement controls to prevent outputs from reproducing copyrighted works, generating trademark-infringing content, or violating third-party intellectual property rights. | AT+EI | Copyright/trademark protection test results. | 1 | 4 | B | EU AI Act Art. 53(1)(c); OECD AI Principle 1.2 | S,A,C | Copyright protection policy; output filtering for copyrighted content; trademark violation test results | Information Governance | EU AI Act Art. 53(1)(c); OECD AI Principle 1.2 | Quarterly | Policy review + basic copyright filtering evidence | Policy + adversarial copyright extraction testing + continuous monitoring | P
ACR-5.16 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system operator SHALL maintain documentation of training data sources, licensing status, consent mechanisms, and provenance chain for all data used in model training and fine-tuning. | EI | Training data provenance documentation; licensing records. | 1 | 4 | B | EU AI Act Art. 10; NIST AI RMF Map 2.3; ISO 42001 A.7.2; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | Training data inventory; per-source licensing documentation; consent records; provenance chain documentation | Information Governance | EU AI Act Art. 10; NIST AI RMF Map 2.3; ISO 42001 A.7.2 | At-Certification | Training data inventory + licensing summary review | Full inventory + per-source licensing verification + consent audit | P
ACR-5.17 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL implement controls to detect and mitigate training data contamination, poisoning, and integrity violations that could compromise data privacy protections. | AT+EI | Data integrity monitoring configuration; contamination detection test results. | 2 | 4 | B | MITRE ATLAS AML.T0020; NIST AI RMF Measure 2.7; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | A,C | Data integrity monitoring pipeline; contamination detection test results; poisoning attack simulation results | Information Governance | MITRE ATLAS AML.T0020; NIST AI RMF Measure 2.7 | Annual | N/A (L2+ only) | Integrity monitoring + contamination testing + poisoning simulation results | P
ACR-5.18 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL resist adversarial attempts to extract training data, system prompts, or confidential information through prompt injection, context manipulation, or repeated querying patterns. | AT | Data exfiltration resistance test results. | 1 | 5 | B | MITRE ATLAS AML.T0024; OWASP LLM-01; NIST AI RMF Measure 2.7; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | F,S,A,C | Adversarial data extraction test suite results; prompt injection resistance for data exfiltration; system prompt protection testing | Information Governance | MITRE ATLAS AML.T0024; OWASP LLM-01; NIST AI RMF Measure 2.7 | Quarterly | Basic extraction resistance testing | Comprehensive adversarial extraction testing + red-team evaluation + continuous monitoring | P
ACR-5.19 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system operator SHALL document data processing locations, data residency compliance, subprocessor relationships, and cross-border data transfer mechanisms. | EI | Data processing location documentation; subprocessor registry. | 1 | 3 | C | GDPR Art. 28; EU AI Act Art. 11; NIST SP 800-53 SA-9; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | Data processing location inventory; subprocessor registry; cross-border transfer mechanism documentation | Information Governance | GDPR Art. 28; EU AI Act Art. 11; NIST SP 800-53 SA-9 | Annual | Documentation review | Documentation + subprocessor audit + transfer mechanism verification | P
ACR-5.20 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL enforce data residency requirements and cross-border transfer restrictions as defined in the system's data processing documentation and applicable regulatory requirements. | AT+EI | Data residency enforcement configuration; transfer restriction test results. | 2 | 4 | B | GDPR Art. 44-49; NIST SP 800-53 SA-9; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | A,C | Data residency enforcement configuration; geographic routing test results; transfer restriction verification | Information Governance | GDPR Art. 44-49; NIST SP 800-53 SA-9 | Annual | N/A (L2+ only) | Enforcement config + geographic routing testing + transfer restriction verification | P
ACR-5.21 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL support data subject rights including access, rectification, erasure, portability, and restriction of processing as required by applicable privacy regulations. | AT+EI | Data subject rights implementation; workflow test results. | 1 | 4 | B | GDPR Art. 15-22; CCPA Sec. 1798.100-125; NIST Privacy Framework ID.IM-P2; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | Data subject rights workflow documentation; access/erasure/portability test results; response time metrics | Information Governance | GDPR Art. 15-22; CCPA Sec. 1798.100-125; NIST Privacy Framework ID.IM-P2 | Annual | Rights workflow documentation + basic testing | Workflow + comprehensive rights testing + response time validation + audit trail | P
ACR-5.22 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system operator SHALL maintain a documented Data Privacy Impact Assessment (DPIA) identifying privacy risks, mitigation measures, and residual risk acceptance for the autonomous system. | EI | Completed DPIA document with risk register. | 1 | 3 | C | GDPR Art. 35; EU AI Act Art. 9; NIST AI RMF Map 1.6; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | Data Privacy Impact Assessment document; privacy risk register; mitigation implementation evidence | Information Governance | GDPR Art. 35; EU AI Act Art. 9; NIST AI RMF Map 1.6 | Annual | DPIA document review | DPIA + mitigation implementation verification + residual risk acceptance documentation | P
ACR-5.23 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system operator SHALL maintain vendor due diligence documentation for upstream model and data providers covering their data handling, PII controls, training data sourcing, and subprocessor relationships. | EI | Vendor due diligence package; provider assessment records. | 1 | 3 | C | NIST AI RMF Map 5.2; ISO 27001 A.5.19-21; NIST SP 800-53 SA-12; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | Vendor due diligence questionnaire responses; provider data handling assessment; subprocessor disclosure records | Information Governance | NIST AI RMF Map 5.2; ISO 27001 A.5.19-21; NIST SP 800-53 SA-12 | Annual | Due diligence documentation review | Documentation + provider assessment validation + periodic re-assessment evidence | P
ACR-5.24 | Domain 5: Data Privacy and Information Protection | The system SHALL maintain data breach detection capabilities and the operator SHALL maintain documented notification procedures for data incidents affecting personal or confidential information. | AT+EI | Breach detection configuration; notification procedure documentation; incident response test results. | 1 | 5 | A | GDPR Art. 33-34; NIST SP 800-53 IR-6; ISO 27001 A.5.24-28; CoSAI Secure-by-Design Agentic Systems (informative) | S,A,C | Breach detection system documentation; notification procedure runbook; tabletop exercise results; notification timeline evidence | Information Governance | GDPR Art. 33-34; NIST SP 800-53 IR-6; ISO 27001 A.5.24-28 | Annual | Procedure documentation + detection system review | Procedures + detection testing + tabletop exercise + notification timeline verification | P

=== SHEET: D6 Failure Mode Containmen ===

ACR-6.01 | Domain 6: Failure Mode Containment | The system SHALL detect outputs that deviate from expected distributions by more than defined thresholds. | AT+CM | Anomaly detection test results. | 1 | 4 | B | NIST AI RMF Measure 2.6 | S,A,C | Anomaly detection test results. | Operational Resilience | NIST AI RMF Measure 2.6 | Annual | Basic automated testing + evidence review | Comprehensive automated testing + continuous monitoring | Y

ACR-6.03 | Domain 6: Failure Mode Containment | The system SHALL escalate critical failures to human operators with sufficient context for informed intervention. | AT+HS | Escalation test results with context completeness verification. | 1 | 5 | B | NIST AI RMF Manage 4.1; EU AI Act Art. 14; NIST AI Agent Standards Initiative (informative) | F,S,A,C | Escalation test results with context completeness verification. | Operational Resilience | NIST AI RMF Manage 4.1; EU AI Act Art. 14 | Quarterly | Basic automated testing + evidence review | Comprehensive automated testing + adversarial simulation + third-party validation | Y

ACR-14.24 | Domain 14: Operational Governance Controls | The deploying organization SHALL notify the platform vendor and ARAF within 14 days of any deployment-side configuration change that affects inherited ACR coverage. Changes that invalidate inherited coverage SHALL trigger a delta evaluation of affected ACRs. | EI+OP | Configuration change notification records; delta evaluation documentation. | 1 | 3 | B | ARA Standard v1.1 §6.2; ARAF Platform Cert Specification v1.0 | S,A,C | Configuration change notification records; delta evaluation documentation. | Governance & Societal Impact | ARA Standard v1.1 §6.2; ARAF Platform Cert Specification v1.0 | Annual | Documentation review + policy inspection | Documentation audit + operational evidence review | P
ACR-14.25 | Domain 14: Operational Governance Controls | If the deploying organization materially changes the system's operational context in a manner that would increase the Risk Classification (e.g., expanding from internal to customer-facing deployment, adding life-safety use cases, or entering a regulated domain), the organization SHALL notify ARAF and the evaluating AVB within 14 days. The AVB SHALL conduct a Risk Classification reassessment to determine whether the Assurance Class must be elevated. | EI+OP | Operational context change notification records; Risk Classification reassessment documentation. | 1 | 4 | A | ARA Standard v1.1 §4.2, §6.2; ARAF Risk Classification Framework | S,A,C | Operational context change notification records; Risk Classification reassessment documentation. | Governance & Societal Impact | ARA Standard v1.1 §4.2, §6.2; ARAF Risk Classification Framework | Annual | Documentation review + policy inspection | Documentation audit + operational evidence review | N

=== SHEET: Scoping Matrix ===

ARA System Profile Scoping Matrix |  |  |  |  | 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 |  |  |  |  | 
Capability Dimension | Description | Foundational (F) | Standard (S) | Advanced (A) | Comprehensive (C)
Deployment | Where is the system deployed? | Internal only | Internal + external | External, multi-org | External, critical infrastructure
Modality | What input/output types? | Text only | Text + structured data | Text + voice/image | All modalities + physical
Tool Access | What can the system invoke? | None | Read-only APIs | Read-write APIs | Administrative + physical actuators
Data Sensitivity | What data does it process? | Public data only | Business confidential | Regulated (PII/PHI/PCI) | Classified or CBRN-adjacent
Autonomy Level | How independently does it act? | Human approves every action | Bounded autonomy, exceptions escalated | High autonomy, spot checks | Full autonomy, safety-critical
Agent Architecture | How many agents? | Single agent | Single agent + tools | Multi-agent orchestration | Multi-agent + physical systems
Regulatory Exposure | What regulations apply? | None/minimal | Standard (GDPR/CCPA) | Sector-specific (HIPAA/FCRA) | High-risk EU AI Act + sector
Impact Scope | Who is affected? | Internal users only | Customers/partners | Public at scale | Safety-critical populations
 |  |  |  |  | 
 |  |  |  |  | 
Scoping Rule: The system profile is determined by the HIGHEST applicable level across all capability dimensions. |  |  |  |  | 
 |  |  |  |  | 
ACR Applicability by Profile |  |  |  |  | 
Profile | Applicable ACRs | Description |  |  | 
Foundational (F) | 99 | Core safety and governance controls. Startup-accessible. |  |  | 
Standard (S) | 225 | Full enterprise controls including data privacy and tool governance. |  |  | 
Advanced (A) | 380 | All digital controls including adversarial robustness and societal impact. |  |  | 
Comprehensive (C) | 410 | All controls including physical systems. Full standard coverage. |  |  |
